font-weight: 600; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.3; margin: 0px;"><span style="font-style:italic;font-weight:600" data-token-index="0" class="notion-enable-hover">Can we override static methods?</span></h4></div></div><div data-block-id="1d784fed-ec1a-4839-9888-4b0c1fa176a9" class="notion-selectable notion-text-block" style="width: 100%; max-width: 1044px; margin-top: 1px; margin-bottom: 1px;"><div style="color: inherit; fill: inherit;"><div style="display: flex;"><div spellcheck="true" placeholder=" " data-content-editable-leaf="true" contenteditable="false" style="max-width: 100%; width: 100%; white-space: pre-wrap; word-break: break-word; caret-color: rgb(55, 53, 47); padding: 3px 2px;"><span style="font-weight:600" data-token-index="0" class="notion-enable-hover">No, we cannot override static methods</span></div></div></div></div><div data-block-id="1f779c6f-f99e-45b5-ac88-7ed1e271b6a8" class="notion-selectable notion-text-block" style="width: 100%; max-width: 1044px; margin-top: 1px; margin-bottom: 1px;"><div style="color: inherit; fill: inherit;"><div style="display: flex;"><div spellcheck="true" placeholder=" " data-content-editable-leaf="true" contenteditable="false" style="max-width: 100%; width: 100%; white-space: pre-wrap; word-break: break-word; caret-color: rgb(55, 53, 47); padding: 3px 2px;">&nbsp;because method overriding is based on dynamic binding at runtime and the static methods are bonded using static binding at compile time. So, we cannot override static methods. The calling of method depends upon the type of object that calls the static method.</div></div></div></div><div data-block-id="60d085fb-6e62-419b-9fcf-cc5dccbaddf5" class="notion-selectable notion-text-block" style="width: 100%;
